Introduction1.

1 PurposeThis Software Requirements Specification (SRS) defines the complete functional and non-functional requirements for TeachLink Africa.

It is the authoritative reference document for product, engineering, design, and QA teams throughout all development phases.

1.

2 Project OverviewTeachLink Africa is a premium two-sided marketplace connecting verified African teachers with local and international parents and students for private and home tutoring.

The platform operates across web and mobile, supports multi-currency transactions, integrates live session infrastructure with time-clocking, and includes an AI-powered teacher upskilling academy.

It competes directly with Preply, Superprof, AmazingTalker, TeacherOn, and Cambly.

1.

3 Platform ModulesMarketplace: Teacher discovery, vetting, booking, and paymentSession Engine: Live classes, time-clocking, recording, and assignment managementAI Academy: Six-module teacher upskilling programme (Google AI Studio / Gemini)Parent Intelligence Dashboard: Real-time progress monitoring and AI insightsReputation Engine: Ratings, badges, leaderboard, and trust signals1.

1 AA4.

5 Scalability and InternationalisationFirestore horizontal scaling supports growth without architectural changes.

All media assets served via CDN (Cloudinary CDN / Firebase CDN) for global latency reduction.

Firebase Cloud Functions process all webhooks, payouts, and scheduled jobs asynchronously.

Backend architecture supports React Native mobile app (Phase 6) without changes.

Gemini API usage shall be rate-limited and batched to stay within Google AI Studio quotas.

Default language: English.

Planned: French (Phase 6), Swahili, Yoruba, Hausa (later phases).

All timestamps stored in UTC; displayed in the user&apos;s detected local timezone.

Platform shall support RTL text rendering for future Arabic language support.

5.

Database Schema (Firebase Firestore)All collections use Firestore document-based NoSQL storage.

Firestore Row-Level Security rules must be applied to every collection.

Acceptance Criteria8.

1 Phase 1 Acceptance CriteriaA teacher completes full onboarding (all steps) in under 10 minutes without encountering any errors.

A parent can search, view a teacher profile, and complete a booking with payment in under 5 minutes.

Payment confirmation email is received by both parties within 60 seconds of successful payment.

Admin can approve or reject a teacher application from the admin dashboard with reason logged.

Teacher profile page achieves a Google Lighthouse SEO score of 90 or above.

All form validation errors display clear, specific, actionable messages.

Platform renders correctly on mobile at 375px width with no horizontal scrollbar.

All payments process in test mode with zero failed transactions on valid cards.

8.

2 Phase 2 Acceptance CriteriaSession clock starts within 5 seconds of both parties joining the video room.

Clock pauses within 10 seconds of a participant disconnecting.

Billed duration matches clock log total active time to within 1 second precision.

Recording is accessible via private URL within 5 minutes of session ending.

Recording URL is inaccessible (returns 403) after 30 days.

Teacher payout triggers automatically 24 hours after session completion with no dispute filed.

Assignment grade notification reaches parent within 60 seconds of teacher submitting grade.

Clock log entries cannot be created or modified by client-side code (Firestore rules verified).

8.

3 General Platform Acceptance CriteriaAll pages pass WCAG 2.

1 AA compliance check via axe-core audit tool with zero critical violations.

No Personally Identifiable Information (PII) appears in browser console logs or network request logs.

All Firestore security rules pass a full rules unit test suite: unauthenticated users cannot read or write protected collections.

All API keys and secrets are stored as environment variables and absent from the git repository (verified via git-secrets scan).

GEMINI_API_KEY is not present in any client-side JavaScript bundle (verified via webpack bundle analysis).

All currency calculations produce results equal to manual minor-unit calculation with zero rounding error on a test suite of 1,000 transactions.

Platform achieves Core Web Vitals &quot;Good&quot; rating (LCP &lt;2.

5s, FID &lt;100ms, CLS &lt;0.

1) on mobile 4G simulation.

Full rules file lives in /firestore.

rules in the repository.

rules_version = &apos;2&apos;;match /teachers/{id} { allow read: if true; allow write: if request.

auth.

uid == id; }match /sessions/{id} { allow read: if request.

auth.

uid == resource.

data.

teacherId || request.

auth.

uid == resource.

data.

parentId; }match /reviews/{id} { allow read: if true; allow create: if request.

auth.

uid == request.

resource.

data.

parentId; }NOTE: Clock log entries in sessions documents must be written by Firebase Cloud Functions only.

Firestore rules must reject any client attempting to write clockLog[] directly.
